0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：be willing to do XX 乐意[愿意] 做某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">willing adj. 愿意的，乐意的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">willing to</span></em></strong> help.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我非常<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">愿意</strong>帮忙。</p><p href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653536064&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=5e5ee62d64287a1e3af7aed36602d4d8&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. <strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：</strong>show / express one's appreciation 表达感激/感谢</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">shows</span></em></strong> little <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">appreciation</span></em></strong> of good music.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">感受</strong>不到美好音乐的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">妙处</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Children rarely <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">show</span></em></strong> any <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">appreciation</span></em></strong> of/for what their parents do for them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孩子对父母为自己所做的一切鲜少<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">表现出感激之情</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</strong></span>Don't forget to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">show</span></em></strong> your <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">appreciation</span></em></strong> for that thing or for that person.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不要忘记对那件事或那个人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">表达</strong>你的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">感激</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">show</span></em></strong> my <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">appreciation</span></em></strong> by sending some big emoji here.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我要发个大表情来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">表达</strong>我的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">感激。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. <strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：through the lens of... 通过...的视角 /从...的角度审视或判断...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He watches everything <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">through the lens of</span></em></strong> his video camera.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">透过</strong>摄像机<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的镜头</strong>观察所有事物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Review your products and services <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">through the lens of</span></em></strong> profitability.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从</strong>盈利能力<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">角度</strong>审视产品和服务。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: seen </span></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">through the lens of </span></em></strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">the working poor.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a vegan-friendly city. </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Very very vegan-friendly. It's almost like...I mean if you're speaking to another foreigner anyway, it's almost like unusual with someone says that they're not vegan or at least vegetarian because there's just so many and there’s vegan restaurants everywhere. And even if it's not a vegan restaurant, and especially in the main city, even if it's not a vegan restaurant, they'll have like separate vegan options. This is really<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> well catered for (很好地满足需求 😌 ) </strong>here. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So can you describe me normally how your meals are like for a day, starting from breakfast? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah. Well in the morning I usually make like smoothie bowl (水果奶昔). Here in Thailand, it's hot all the time. So it's really refreshing in the morning and I love fruit. I can never eat too much fruit. So I make smoothie bowls like frozen banana and I just make it differently every day. </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfuQfibTeibia9HJBDLnQ2ezY2krlFpwp2o2NHTVHhlz1J6qWRuKAs46RsA4qQSW26XJ4g5aTOg42dYA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Like frozen banana and I like sweet potato and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cocoa powder (可可粉)</strong> make it like a chocolate one or and I put strawberries in it and make it like a fruity one. And I always put in lots of different <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">toppings (糕点上的配料)</strong> like <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">flax seeds （亚麻籽)</strong>, really essential for vegans to have every day. So <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ground (磨碎的)</strong> flax seeds I always put in.  I just like different <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">superfoods (超级食品，一些人认为有益健康且可防病的食品) </strong>in the morning. And lunchtime I usually have a salad. And in the evening like porridge or like a<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> stew (炖煮的菜肴) </strong>or like cooked potatoes as well. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I could go out, but because I try to avoid too much oil and salt. I like to go out and I mean anything like a vegan burger or whatever and it’s always vegan, pasta, pizza.</em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfuQfibTeibia9HJBDLnQ2ezY2BichCjtmzqEKASgv2QrFVltMfsxZR1dRDI2407jiaoGUiaWRr7VgouF3g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/fhyp8NkR0JbWTK76Uq4XbGT5Muoasfm3szmPQug3SutXPvgJtVsic7JQTwiawIVicwM4ibNDfY1ISgSdWtMcbiaxm8A/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Actually  I'm eating less meat nowadays. I consider it healthy.</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, a lot of people nowadays are cutting out meat for that reason. I mean for me, it wasn't about health at all when I first became a vegetarian. It wasn't on my mind as a little kid but more in the adult life, I’ve become more interested in the health side and I find that people tend to…in fact nowadays vegan has become more popular for that reason. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">In the news, you hear a lot of information about the dangers of meat and like number one<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> carcinogen (致癌物), </strong>and same with eggs and dairy. It’s really focused at the moment. It’s so technical right now I think diet and eating meat. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So where did you get the protein? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Protein actually is the one thing that's in everything, people don't realize that protein is in almost everything, vegetables, beans, tofu. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> It’s not something to worry about. If you do like a test, I’ve never ever had a problem. You never hear of anybody having protein deficiency. It’s more like…calcium is quite hard because you have to eat a really high volume of…You can get<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> calcium (钙) </strong>from vegetables but you have to eat a high volume of them to get the same amount that you would in dairy. So the easiest answer is to eat foods that have forty-five calcium in them like <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">soy milk (豆乳)</strong>, for example, most soy milk has a forty-five calcium in it.</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">So there's ways like that. And vitamin B12, it has to be a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">tablet (片剂)</strong>, because there is no plant source of B12. So that’s the only thing that vegans can't get naturally from their diet. So it has to be a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">supplement (营养片剂)</strong>, just a tablet. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 6px solid transparent !important;border-left: 5px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All work and no play makes Jack a dull boy.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">只工作不玩耍，聪明孩子也会变傻</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All play and no work makes Greg a playboy.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">只会玩不工作，自律的人也会变花花公子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Go on holiday =go on vacation/take a vacation去度假；正在休假</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Where am I gonna go on holiday, that's a decisive moment.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我该去哪里度假，这就是个决定性的时刻。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">free</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/friː/ US/fri/(adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①Someone or something that is free is not restricted, controlled, or limited, for example, by rules, customs, or other people. 自由的; 不受限制的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个列子：To be free? But are we really free?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们追求着所谓的自由，可是我们真的自由吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②If something is free, you can have it or use it without paying for it. 免费的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Ice bear will have more free chips.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">北极熊还要点免费薯条。---《咱们裸熊》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">③free and easy(adj.)natural and unstudied无拘无束的，不拘礼节的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Life was never going to be so free and easy again.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">生活绝不会再那样无拘无束了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">④not containing something: not containing a particular thing (often used in combination)不含../没有...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：a salt-free diet无盐餐</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Duty-free store免税商店</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Alcohol-free不含酒精</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Go(went)away take vacation: to leave the border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UNCLE ANDREW and his study vanished instantly. Then, for a moment, everything became muddled. The next thing Digory knew was that there was a soft green light coming down on him from above, and darkness below. He didn't seem to be standing on anything, or sitting, or lying. Nothing appeared to be touching him. "I believe I'm in water," said Digory. "Or under water." This frightened him for a second, but almost at once he could feel that he was rushing upwards. Then his head suddenly came out into the air and, he found himself scrambling ashore, out on to smooth grassy ground at the edge of a pool.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">安德鲁舅舅和他的书房立刻消失了。之后的一刹那，四周昏暗而迷茫。接着，迪格雷感到，头顶上射来一束柔和的绿光，下面一片漆黑。他似乎既未站在什么上面，也未坐在或躺在什么上面，四周空空如也。“我相信自己在水中。”迪格雷说，“要么在水下。”这使他吓了一跳，但他马上就觉得在往上冲。突然，他的脑袋接触到空气，他发现自己钻了出来，在水潭边平坦的碧草地上趴着。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 最近你父母身体好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 哦，都很好。他们依然很活跃，退休生活过得很愉快。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那太好了，这真让人高兴。你回家时请代我向他们问好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 一定，谢谢你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How are your parents these days?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Oh, they're fine, still very active and enjoying their retirement.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Oh, good. That's nice to hear. Please give my best regards to them when you're home.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Sure, thank you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't figure out how to break the news to them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我_________怎么把这事跟他们说。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">想不出</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿: instead of XX / doing XX 代替…；而不是…</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Instead of</span></em></strong> being annoyed, he seemed quite pleased.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有</strong>生气，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">反而</strong>似乎很高兴。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Now I can walk to work <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">instead of</span></em></strong> going by car.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在我可以步行去上班，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">而不</strong>必开车了。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>We treat it like a nice-to-have <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">instead of</span></em></strong> a must-have.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们把它当作是一件值得拥有的东西，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">而不是</strong>一件必须拥有的东西。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>Your biological stress response is <span style="text-decoration: underline;">nudging</span> you to tell someone how you feel, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">instead of</span></em></strong> <span style="text-decoration: underline;">bottling it up</span>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">生理应激反应促使你告诉别人你的感受<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">而不是</strong>把它憋在心里。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Let me call it height <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">instead of</span></em></strong> y.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们用高度来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">代替</strong>y。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1515.91px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 1515.91px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 1515.91px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 1515.91px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿: be on one's </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">own</g></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 单独地，独自地</strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’ve <span style="color: rgb(22, 21, 21);box-sizing: border-box;">been</span> living <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">on my own</span></em></strong> for four years now.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我已经<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">独自</strong>生活了四年。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can <span style="text-decoration: underline;">manage <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自己</strong>能行，谢谢。</p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">by oneself</strong> </p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Found your <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">own </g>apartment, did it all <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">on your own</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">找到了自己的公寓，赚钱付房租。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">昨晚和好友义通电话，一提及我每日早读的事儿，我的嘴里像是装了无数发子弹，噼里啪啦讲个不停。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当晚，到睡觉时间，我闭着眼躺在床上，以为会和往常一般，快速进入睡眠状态。哪能料想，一沾枕头，脑袋就开始飞速旋转，所有的一切都在围绕着早读不断地蔓延，大脑处于一种持续兴奋的状态中，无法控制。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大概很久之后的睡着，还是和以前的某些夜晚相同，是因为<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">回想起某个清晨的早读句子</strong>，然后慢慢回忆着💤</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在很难入睡的昨晚（2021年8月9日晚），原本想放纵一夜自己的眼睛，跳下床，拿起手机查看自己早读的点滴，再打开电脑，记录自己早读的大致过程与所有快乐，思考一二，担心自己的眼睛不乖，加上自身胆小如鼠，便退想，最好的时机会来。那时，大脑该比此时更兴奋，我也便可一气呵成自己与早读的全过程，也就无需现在找勇气与黑夜抗衡。于是，继续闭眼，享受着有关早读占据着整个大脑。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 1 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">初次相逢</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">初次相逢TeacherGwen早读，能让我想起我的挚友玉儿，在她早读打卡20天左右的日子，也就是2018年5月底6月初这段时间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在想来或许是个巧合，因为玉儿的生日就在这时间内，我点开她分享的圈圈链接，先听一遍早读、感受句子的意思、学造句、看留言等等，最后找了一个笔记本，写下当天早读。<span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接着，开始回看玉儿之前分享的早读圈圈链接，兴趣使我在当天看了Gwen老师更早的推送。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">往后的日子，我每天听着老师的声音，在笔记本上面记录着老师的分享，翻阅自己的圈圈，我发现自己偶尔会使用Gwen老师分享的句子来表达自己当下心情：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.375" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfgNSDz0r6xE4QzichV69E4gsIpEjVNwlQK2miau50PXhLDH7o1IDWDgbQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直到2018年10月12日，以这条圈圈为始：</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.0101010101010102" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANf8oLhjeUpQian2e8ofpltNmEIkCiaZ8twdMZgOpGab6dkKqH7qqZibZ4Ow/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="792" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">开始持续在圈圈分享Gwen老师的早读，所以，我以这条圈圈为界，心里把初逢TeacherGwen到这条圈圈，作为遇到Gwen老师的第一阶段。分享的内容，大致都是这样的形式:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.5594541910331383" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANf5ZBINt68GLxVGberFBJiaqcuZFicmia9mLOUVxImLgWGleeeicIEUWJ7og/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="513" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没有分享链接，就是学习后，把来源、句子、知识点和自己的造句分享到圈圈，现在想起来，好像自己偷用了Gwen老师的学习资源，没有写明真正的出处是来自我喜欢的TeacherGwen公众号。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 2 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“偷”用资源</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">回想偷用资源分享的这段日子，我的学习与生活是如此的充实，每日清晨伴随着Gwen老师温柔有力的声音，或是手握笔头静静的守候在电脑与手机旁，或是戴着耳机微笑漫步在路间，又或是快步去往餐厅与操场的路上……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时至今日，我还能清晰想起那段日子里的学过一些句子，因为Gwen老师的分享，很多时候能够恰到好处，深入内心，带的给我勇气和安慰，以前常常看TeacherGwen每日早读公众号下的留言，看别人的造句与感谢，发现我和许多人一样有着相同的感觉，就是Gwen老师的早读句子，能够植入我们的内心。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">写到这里，脑袋突然想起Gwen老师分享的一些句子:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“你爱的人能改变你，你学的知识能指引你”，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"我喜欢的是你，你的一分一毫，你的皮肤，你的眼睛，你的感受，无论新旧"，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“大胆生活，积极上进，别过于安逸”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">太多太多了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对第二个句子尤其深刻，那时我正简简单单的喜欢着一个简单认真的男孩子，当天的圈圈我特意做了一张精致的图，让它能与这么美好的句子一起出现在圈圈里:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.098901098901099" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfyU8DQo0pML5ic7YVOhLvXCFUXiaulsdQYetrfibhYRskia1S14sTK4XGDw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="728" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">偷用资源的这段日子，还有一个画面会偶至脑中。那便是，晚上和亲密好友同到操场运动时，我必定会将当天的英语早读句子从我的脑袋里拿出，再从嘴里分享给她们，分享所涉及的单词拼写、单词发音、哪些单词的音难发易错、该句子还能如何翻译……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我会想起盟猪宝、小枫、敏哥哥、未来作家霞霞，这四位善于倾听的大学亲密好友，总能在我分享时，将她们一双可爱的耳朵和一颗真诚的心送给我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大脑多次回忆、嘴中不断输出当天的句子，使得我对当日句子更加深刻。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在之后考英语四六级作文时，句子一股脑全部浮现</strong>，是多么的快乐啊！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大学这四年，承载着我生命中无数美好的记忆，她们以及其他挚友伙伴们带给我事物很多，不仅于此。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 3 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">加入早读班</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">某一天，也就是2019年4月8日，我开始以另外一种方式分享我的每日早读:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.72875" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfu2YdGlcEiaM9ViciazcGkS4MpFJAByFuibZS5KE0UBDLovG6HALnzRnxng/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为我怀着好奇与想要学习的心成功进入了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">早读班级</strong>，我想知道在Gwen老师这个大家庭下的班级是什么样的。我会有这样的猜想：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">会不会是水群？</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">会不会交什么费用？</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">带着这个疑问，进群后，群规则过于多、过于详细，使得我有些乱麻。现在已经是在在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">早读群里打卡的855天，听写群里打卡的397天</strong>。自我回答内心的疑惑，群没有一滴水，群与费用没有关系，就是许许多多热爱英语、想要学好英语的人。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">无比幸运的地遇见了一个叫TeacherGwen公众号，经过号里分享的学习资源，然后怀着想要学习英语的心，最终与这个大家庭相融在一起。这些人，来自各行各业，有老师、外卖小哥、IT人员、宝妈、会计……，有上至高龄八十好几的爷爷奶奶们，下至四五岁的小宝宝们，也有许多如我一样的学生，还有身居国外的人，这许多人跨时间，跨地域，跨年龄，共同出现在Gwen老师这里，跟着Gwen老师一起，每天都进步一点点。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">往后我回想规则，其实特别清晰，由衷佩服各个班级里的学委班班们，每天自觉自愿免费管理上百人的群，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">细致到哪个同学截图或语音或打卡号有问题。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">群里每天会有纠音名额，早起的我得到纠音名额是一定的，我不满足于此，还要得到自己最喜欢的班班纠音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Alex班班是我进第一个早读群里最喜欢的班班，他的声音很好听，善于捕捉我语音中出现的问题，讲解容易理解，让我纠正自己错音变得容易。我用记事本记下在早读群里因为发音进步或者发音到位得到班班的各种表扬。然后，快乐地放进我的百天总结里:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我就这样记录了我的三个百天，这是第二个百天:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看到自己在Alex班班那里得到的花花、皇冠和表扬，真快乐:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在正在第九个百天的途中，没有再记录自己所得到的表扬，但依旧每天争取优秀。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">分享快乐</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen老师早读的句子来源十分广泛，有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">歌曲、电影、电视剧、演讲、古诗文</strong>等等，因此我会记录下自己想看的电影或电视剧、想反复听的诗歌、想重复观看的演讲。于是，我带着无比愉悦的心情，看了喜欢的电影，在电影中能下意识的关注一些常用的表达。观影后，我会分享自己的快乐:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为每天的早读，慢慢地开始阅读一些简单有趣的英文书籍，每次阅读完一本，都忍不住要在圈圈分享:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1251758087201125" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfpz1zfwiapicFVty3fl8CGGib5xpYnxBYdTOETUwxGHpssLeEosjv1c8IA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="711" 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那种分享的感觉，就是特别想让看到的人，也喜欢上这本书，并产生去读或了解这本书的冲动。总之，过程特别快乐，现在回想依旧如初:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="2.4691358024691357" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfsicr7Tn0CZ9HiaI2FvXMSiaoB4lLrWBewMFVxxFPw5dsB6dx1kNyS5R2Q/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="324" border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 5 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">万般美好，已然在心中</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有幸入过Gwen老师的音标课、口语课、语音语调课。当时收到课本的我总是激动得不成样子:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.87625" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfo5Tgw9QOxAnDZsIRAcDr0oEWlsjyypRnqibXicUibUYkwmqRqGjvJzC6A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每次课，都能遇到温柔的班班们，她们的细致入微让我觉得这世界上优秀而又独具魅力的人真多。我的音标班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Rasina</strong>，口语班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">娜娜</strong>，语音语调班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">小野马</strong>，这些班班啊，我不知道该如何形容...... <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">优秀、温柔、很热爱生活，她们嘴里出来的每个单词，每个句子，都像是唱歌儿般，如此动听。偶尔发呆时，会问自己何时也能在话从口出时，如同歌儿一样动听呢？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">还记得音标课前，傻傻幻想着在银屏上见到Gwen老师的场景，以及口语课前，痴痴的想象着在屏幕看到Gwen老师的时候，到语音语调课时，是在大脑里通过Gwen老师的声音和她公众号所有分享的知识，来勾勒Gwen老师的样子，想着Gwen老师的时候，细心、认真、善良、独立、有爱心、有思想等等词汇与Gwen老师联系在一起，但已经不再期待从什么设备中看到Gwen老师了，因为万般美好，已然在心中。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 6 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“纠音班长”之梦</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">突然想说，不知何时，我心中一直有个梦，哈哈哈，这样说，有些好笑。在2019年时希望自己也能成为一个早读班的纠音班班，并为之着手努力，抓住机会参加过选拔。当然，失败告终。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2020年，我在笔记本上，写下了当年的目标，其中之一是成为一名纠音班班，但我没有抓住机会，因为我觉得自己的水平还远远不及能够帮助到别人的地步。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2021年，我依旧有这个目标，与上一年不同，今年的我，勇气可嘉。五月份，抓住机会参加了选拔，因为通过选拔进入实习期，心中持续兴奋了一周左右:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.702127659574468" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfUUiaFqcFwZGy9ld7bFxo0gjHiceABLuOcXegFpBUt4t7icF12ibnwpN6Zg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="470" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但实习还没结束，途中被告知没有通过，多少有些难受。但是一想到实习里的日子，满是收获，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">小五</strong>班班给我的许多指导，在后面的早读中一直使我收益，这是我没有实习前无法获得的，倍感欣慰。在实习中认识了实习班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Luna</strong>，她很有闯劲，我们偶尔会有英语学习的交流，相互鼓励，争取抓住下次机会。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第二次机会来啦，我两次都顺利地进入了实习班级，现仍在实习中。这次我遇到的实习师傅是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">颜颜</strong>，她总是腾出时间来指导我和另外一个实习班班。为人非常随和，交流问题没有任何拘束感，这大概就是Gwen老师团队下面优秀人的共同特点吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">目前，对自己实习任务的完成还算比较满意，也希望自己能够顺利通过实习。当然，如果没有通过也没有关系，因为总有一天会成功的，这一天到来前，我怎么说都不会轻易放弃，就像Gwen老师早读里面的句子一样:"<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">幸运+努力工作，总有一天会成功的</strong>"，"<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完美，是你需要花多长时间投入成就这份完美的事情</strong>"。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 7 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">说不完，道不尽</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">偶尔有同学问我，为什么我那么能坚持，除了真心回答已经习惯或者喜欢Gwen老师做的早读，别的说不出什么原因。说多或者说大了，听起来自己都觉得不舒服，不说或者什么的，又觉得有些娇柔做作。我自己是知道的，因为在这过程中，我感受到了自己的进步，遇到的是一个温暖优秀的大家庭，看到的是许多同样热爱英语而聚集在Gwen老师身旁的人，陪伴我们的学委班班们都有着一颗无私奉献的心，Gwen老师是一个有趣也同样持之以恒，并随时探索学习新点子的老师……这许多的原因，让我理解了之前的分享，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">因为喜欢，无需坚持</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时常翻阅Gwen老师的微博，学习的同时，也兴致勃勃地查看Gwen老师在生活方面的分享与互动，推荐好看的书籍，读有趣的绘画，提出学习和生活上的疑惑见解，分享生活中实用技巧，记录旅途中的心得……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一瞬间想说自己已经跟着Gwen老师很久了，随后一想，又有些不对。往后的日子里，不管学习还是生活，都是要追随着Gwen老师的，往后的时间还很长很长，还会有很多分享想要说给我喜欢的Gwen老师，说给我自己，也说给我的挚友伙伴们，以及我认识和不认识的人们。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">若是没有昨晚的一通电话，不知什么时候才会记录这些点点滴滴，已经到尾声了，还有种说不完，道不尽的感觉，是啊！这又怎么能说得完，道得尽呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">- by 摇曳幸福</p><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2021/8/10</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 10px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">也期待看到你的分享。<span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请将你的早读故事发送给我</span><strong style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（微信号teachergwen02）</strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">。一经采纳，将送出现已绝版的【早读纪念套卡】或【纪念刊】一套。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本栏目长期征稿，每周二发出。</span></p></section>style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">全文字数：   3615</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">阅读时间：   11 分钟</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">图片数目：   15</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 10px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 25px;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: perspective(0px);-webkit-transform: perspective(0px);-moz-transform: perspective(0px);-o-transform: perspective(0px);transform-style: flat;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: rotateX(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateX(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateX(180deg);-o-transform: rotateX(180deg);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 10px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 208, 90);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">昨晚和好友义通电话，一提及我每日早读的事儿，我的嘴里像是装了无数发子弹，噼里啪啦讲个不停。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当晚，到睡觉时间，我闭着眼躺在床上，以为会和往常一般，快速进入睡眠状态。哪能料想，一沾枕头，脑袋就开始飞速旋转，所有的一切都在围绕着早读不断地蔓延，大脑处于一种持续兴奋的状态中，无法控制。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大概很久之后的睡着，还是和以前的某些夜晚相同，是因为<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">回想起某个清晨的早读句子</strong>，然后慢慢回忆着💤</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在很难入睡的昨晚（2021年8月9日晚），原本想放纵一夜自己的眼睛，跳下床，拿起手机查看自己早读的点滴，再打开电脑，记录自己早读的大致过程与所有快乐，思考一二，担心自己的眼睛不乖，加上自身胆小如鼠，便退想，最好的时机会来。那时，大脑该比此时更兴奋，我也便可一气呵成自己与早读的全过程，也就无需现在找勇气与黑夜抗衡。于是，继续闭眼，享受着有关早读占据着整个大脑。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 1 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">初次相逢</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">初次相逢TeacherGwen早读，能让我想起我的挚友玉儿，在她早读打卡20天左右的日子，也就是2018年5月底6月初这段时间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在想来或许是个巧合，因为玉儿的生日就在这时间内，我点开她分享的圈圈链接，先听一遍早读、感受句子的意思、学造句、看留言等等，最后找了一个笔记本，写下当天早读。<span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">接着，开始回看玉儿之前分享的早读圈圈链接，兴趣使我在当天看了Gwen老师更早的推送。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">往后的日子，我每天听着老师的声音，在笔记本上面记录着老师的分享，翻阅自己的圈圈，我发现自己偶尔会使用Gwen老师分享的句子来表达自己当下心情：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing:
