border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直到2018年10月12日，以这条圈圈为始：</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.0101010101010102" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANf8oLhjeUpQian2e8ofpltNmEIkCiaZ8twdMZgOpGab6dkKqH7qqZibZ4Ow/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="792" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">开始持续在圈圈分享Gwen老师的早读，所以，我以这条圈圈为界，心里把初逢TeacherGwen到这条圈圈，作为遇到Gwen老师的第一阶段。分享的内容，大致都是这样的形式:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.5594541910331383" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANf5ZBINt68GLxVGberFBJiaqcuZFicmia9mLOUVxImLgWGleeeicIEUWJ7og/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="513" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没有分享链接，就是学习后，把来源、句子、知识点和自己的造句分享到圈圈，现在想起来，好像自己偷用了Gwen老师的学习资源，没有写明真正的出处是来自我喜欢的TeacherGwen公众号。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 2 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“偷”用资源</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">回想偷用资源分享的这段日子，我的学习与生活是如此的充实，每日清晨伴随着Gwen老师温柔有力的声音，或是手握笔头静静的守候在电脑与手机旁，或是戴着耳机微笑漫步在路间，又或是快步去往餐厅与操场的路上……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时至今日，我还能清晰想起那段日子里的学过一些句子，因为Gwen老师的分享，很多时候能够恰到好处，深入内心，带的给我勇气和安慰，以前常常看TeacherGwen每日早读公众号下的留言，看别人的造句与感谢，发现我和许多人一样有着相同的感觉，就是Gwen老师的早读句子，能够植入我们的内心。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">写到这里，脑袋突然想起Gwen老师分享的一些句子:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“你爱的人能改变你，你学的知识能指引你”，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"我喜欢的是你，你的一分一毫，你的皮肤，你的眼睛，你的感受，无论新旧"，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“大胆生活，积极上进，别过于安逸”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">太多太多了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对第二个句子尤其深刻，那时我正简简单单的喜欢着一个简单认真的男孩子，当天的圈圈我特意做了一张精致的图，让它能与这么美好的句子一起出现在圈圈里:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.098901098901099" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfyU8DQo0pML5ic7YVOhLvXCFUXiaulsdQYetrfibhYRskia1S14sTK4XGDw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="728" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">偷用资源的这段日子，还有一个画面会偶至脑中。那便是，晚上和亲密好友同到操场运动时，我必定会将当天的英语早读句子从我的脑袋里拿出，再从嘴里分享给她们，分享所涉及的单词拼写、单词发音、哪些单词的音难发易错、该句子还能如何翻译……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我会想起盟猪宝、小枫、敏哥哥、未来作家霞霞，这四位善于倾听的大学亲密好友，总能在我分享时，将她们一双可爱的耳朵和一颗真诚的心送给我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大脑多次回忆、嘴中不断输出当天的句子，使得我对当日句子更加深刻。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在之后考英语四六级作文时，句子一股脑全部浮现</strong>，是多么的快乐啊！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大学这四年，承载着我生命中无数美好的记忆，她们以及其他挚友伙伴们带给我事物很多，不仅于此。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 3 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">加入早读班</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">某一天，也就是2019年4月8日，我开始以另外一种方式分享我的每日早读:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.72875" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfu2YdGlcEiaM9ViciazcGkS4MpFJAByFuibZS5KE0UBDLovG6HALnzRnxng/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为我怀着好奇与想要学习的心成功进入了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">早读班级</strong>，我想知道在Gwen老师这个大家庭下的班级是什么样的。我会有这样的猜想：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">会不会是水群？</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">会不会交什么费用？</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">带着这个疑问，进群后，群规则过于多、过于详细，使得我有些乱麻。现在已经是在在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">早读群里打卡的855天，听写群里打卡的397天</strong>。自我回答内心的疑惑，群没有一滴水，群与费用没有关系，就是许许多多热爱英语、想要学好英语的人。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">无比幸运的地遇见了一个叫TeacherGwen公众号，经过号里分享的学习资源，然后怀着想要学习英语的心，最终与这个大家庭相融在一起。这些人，来自各行各业，有老师、外卖小哥、IT人员、宝妈、会计……，有上至高龄八十好几的爷爷奶奶们，下至四五岁的小宝宝们，也有许多如我一样的学生，还有身居国外的人，这许多人跨时间，跨地域，跨年龄，共同出现在Gwen老师这里，跟着Gwen老师一起，每天都进步一点点。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">往后我回想规则，其实特别清晰，由衷佩服各个班级里的学委班班们，每天自觉自愿免费管理上百人的群，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">细致到哪个同学截图或语音或打卡号有问题。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">群里每天会有纠音名额，早起的我得到纠音名额是一定的，我不满足于此，还要得到自己最喜欢的班班纠音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Alex班班是我进第一个早读群里最喜欢的班班，他的声音很好听，善于捕捉我语音中出现的问题，讲解容易理解，让我纠正自己错音变得容易。我用记事本记下在早读群里因为发音进步或者发音到位得到班班的各种表扬。然后，快乐地放进我的百天总结里:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在正在第九个百天的途中，没有再记录自己所得到的表扬，但依旧每天争取优秀。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 4 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">分享快乐</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen老师早读的句子来源十分广泛，有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">歌曲、电影、电视剧、演讲、古诗文</strong>等等，因此我会记录下自己想看的电影或电视剧、想反复听的诗歌、想重复观看的演讲。于是，我带着无比愉悦的心情，看了喜欢的电影，在电影中能下意识的关注一些常用的表达。观影后，我会分享自己的快乐:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.7241379310344827" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfRJIoldj8FuiafkN8ubGuhlLrLslKDv9jZNO9Vw9u95D1wTDwSATjwrA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="464" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那时候的分享心格外强烈，似乎能时时刻刻都能感受到1+1＞2的快乐:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="2.7874564459930316" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfV1YY4hZwYuTv99fdJduhaNicG1wG4dxuGrnmbCDNhUt1AnE3hXDG8aQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="287" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为每天的早读，慢慢地开始阅读一些简单有趣的英文书籍，每次阅读完一本，都忍不住要在圈圈分享:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1251758087201125" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfpz1zfwiapicFVty3fl8CGGib5xpYnxBYdTOETUwxGHpssLeEosjv1c8IA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="711" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那种分享的感觉，就是特别想让看到的人，也喜欢上这本书，并产生去读或了解这本书的冲动。总之，过程特别快乐，现在回想依旧如初:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="2.4691358024691357" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfsicr7Tn0CZ9HiaI2FvXMSiaoB4lLrWBewMFVxxFPw5dsB6dx1kNyS5R2Q/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="324" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 5 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">万般美好，已然在心中</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有幸入过Gwen老师的音标课、口语课、语音语调课。当时收到课本的我总是激动得不成样子:</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.87625" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfo5Tgw9QOxAnDZsIRAcDr0oEWlsjyypRnqibXicUibUYkwmqRqGjvJzC6A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每次课，都能遇到温柔的班班们，她们的细致入微让我觉得这世界上优秀而又独具魅力的人真多。我的音标班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Rasina</strong>，口语班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">娜娜</strong>，语音语调班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">小野马</strong>，这些班班啊，我不知道该如何形容...... <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">优秀、温柔、很热爱生活，她们嘴里出来的每个单词，每个句子，都像是唱歌儿般，如此动听。偶尔发呆时，会问自己何时也能在话从口出时，如同歌儿一样动听呢？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">还记得音标课前，傻傻幻想着在银屏上见到Gwen老师的场景，以及口语课前，痴痴的想象着在屏幕看到Gwen老师的时候，到语音语调课时，是在大脑里通过Gwen老师的声音和她公众号所有分享的知识，来勾勒Gwen老师的样子，想着Gwen老师的时候，细心、认真、善良、独立、有爱心、有思想等等词汇与Gwen老师联系在一起，但已经不再期待从什么设备中看到Gwen老师了，因为万般美好，已然在心中。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 6 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“纠音班长”之梦</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">突然想说，不知何时，我心中一直有个梦，哈哈哈，这样说，有些好笑。在2019年时希望自己也能成为一个早读班的纠音班班，并为之着手努力，抓住机会参加过选拔。当然，失败告终。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2020年，我在笔记本上，写下了当年的目标，其中之一是成为一名纠音班班，但我没有抓住机会，因为我觉得自己的水平还远远不及能够帮助到别人的地步。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2021年，我依旧有这个目标，与上一年不同，今年的我，勇气可嘉。五月份，抓住机会参加了选拔，因为通过选拔进入实习期，心中持续兴奋了一周左右:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.702127659574468" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANfUUiaFqcFwZGy9ld7bFxo0gjHiceABLuOcXegFpBUt4t7icF12ibnwpN6Zg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="470" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但实习还没结束，途中被告知没有通过，多少有些难受。但是一想到实习里的日子，满是收获，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">小五</strong>班班给我的许多指导，在后面的早读中一直使我收益，这是我没有实习前无法获得的，倍感欣慰。在实习中认识了实习班班<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Luna</strong>，她很有闯劲，我们偶尔会有英语学习的交流，相互鼓励，争取抓住下次机会。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第二次机会来啦，我两次都顺利地进入了实习班级，现仍在实习中。这次我遇到的实习师傅是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">颜颜</strong>，她总是腾出时间来指导我和另外一个实习班班。为人非常随和，交流问题没有任何拘束感，这大概就是Gwen老师团队下面优秀人的共同特点吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">目前，对自己实习任务的完成还算比较满意，也希望自己能够顺利通过实习。当然，如果没有通过也没有关系，因为总有一天会成功的，这一天到来前，我怎么说都不会轻易放弃，就像Gwen老师早读里面的句子一样:"<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">幸运+努力工作，总有一天会成功的</strong>"，"<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完美，是你需要花多长时间投入成就这份完美的事情</strong>"。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 7 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">说不完，道不尽</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">偶尔有同学问我，为什么我那么能坚持，除了真心回答已经习惯或者喜欢Gwen老师做的早读，别的说不出什么原因。说多或者说大了，听起来自己都觉得不舒服，不说或者什么的，又觉得有些娇柔做作。我自己是知道的，因为在这过程中，我感受到了自己的进步，遇到的是一个温暖优秀的大家庭，看到的是许多同样热爱英语而聚集在Gwen老师身旁的人，陪伴我们的学委班班们都有着一颗无私奉献的心，Gwen老师是一个有趣也同样持之以恒，并随时探索学习新点子的老师……这许多的原因，让我理解了之前的分享，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">因为喜欢，无需坚持</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时常翻阅Gwen老师的微博，学习的同时，也兴致勃勃地查看Gwen老师在生活方面的分享与互动，推荐好看的书籍，读有趣的绘画，提出学习和生活上的疑惑见解，分享生活中实用技巧，记录旅途中的心得……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一瞬间想说自己已经跟着Gwen老师很久了，随后一想，又有些不对。往后的日子里，不管学习还是生活，都是要追随着Gwen老师的，往后的时间还很长很长，还会有很多分享想要说给我喜欢的Gwen老师，说给我自己，也说给我的挚友伙伴们，以及我认识和不认识的人们。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">若是没有昨晚的一通电话，不知什么时候才会记录这些点点滴滴，已经到尾声了，还有种说不完，道不尽的感觉，是啊！这又怎么能说得完，道得尽呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">- by 摇曳幸福</p><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2021/8/10</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 10px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 25px;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: perspective(0px);-webkit-transform: perspective(0px);-moz-transform: perspective(0px);-o-transform: perspective(0px);transform-style: flat;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: rotateX(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateX(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateX(180deg);-o-transform: rotateX(180deg);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 10px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 208, 90);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">也期待看到你的分享。<span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请将你的早读故事发送给我</span><strong style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（微信号teachergwen02）</strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">。一经采纳，将送出现已绝版的【早读纪念套卡】或【纪念刊】一套。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本栏目长期征稿，每周二发出。</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.262962962962963" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdMrMhSricHsquMPamqbdANf5PubGfx4d7NjO16p9OW7sjqRqMCl5VMKsU1sLQ1cibTHOgttiapcR1Lw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></sectio</section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">as</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adverb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used in comparisons to refer to the degree of something（用于比较）像…（一样），和…（一样）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's not as good as it used to be.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个不如以前好了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Preposition</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used to describe the purpose or quality of someone or something以…的身份；作为</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She works as a waitress.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她是名服务员。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Conjunction</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：because因为，由于</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As it was getting late, I decided to book into a hotel.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为天色已晚，我决定找家旅馆投宿。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：during the time that当…时；在…的同时；随着</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I saw him as I was coming into the building.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我进楼时看到了他。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：in the same way以…的方式；如同…那样；像</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He got divorced, as his parents had done years before.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他离婚了，重蹈了多年前他父母婚姻破裂的覆辙。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：although虽然，尽管</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Angry as he was, he couldn't help smiling.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">尽管他很生气，可还是忍不住笑了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">all work and no play (makes Jack a dull boy)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：said to warn someone that they will not be an interesting person</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> by working all the time只用功不玩耍（聪明孩子也变傻）。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">alone</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：without other people单独（的），独自（的）；孤独的（地），无伴的（地）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He likes being alone in the house.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他喜欢自己一个人呆在家里。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：without any others唯一，仅仅，只有</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She alone needs to decide what to do.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她必须自己决定做什么。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lonely</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：unhappy because you are not with other people孤独的，寂寞的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She gets lonely now that all the kids have left home.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在孩子们都离开了家，她感到有些孤独。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：A lonely place is a long way from where people live.孤独的，孤零零的，远离人群的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a lonely stretch of Arizona highway</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">亚利桑那一段荒凉的公路</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">go for broke</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to risk everything in the hope of having great success孤注一掷</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">go for it</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to do anything you have to in order to get something尽力争取；不遗余力去做</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"I'm thinking of applying for that job." "Go for it!"</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“我正在考虑去应聘那份工作。” “努力去争取吧！”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center center;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: cover;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdvjmW05ZIUpmJqRNXePM74or8LibAKaDTzs2sXpv9bEkwTR7ibSvqt5QRibXPvu5bdJHLvdFoLosnHw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg");overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;'><section style="height: 100%;overflow: hidden;line-height: 0;vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"> <img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdvjmW05ZIUpmJqRNXePM74or8LibAKaDTzs2sXpv9bEkwTR7ibSvqt5QRibXPvu5bdJHLvdFoLosnHw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="200" style="width: 100%;height: 100%;opacity: 0;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);margin: -0.5em 0px 0px;padding-bottom: 0.5em;border-top-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Tuesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">But</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">she adde</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(31, 73, 125);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">I think by Saturday nigh</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As he rose to his feet he noticed that he was neither dripping nor panting for breath as anyone would expect after being under water. His clothes were perfectly dry. He was standing by the edge of a small pool - not more than ten feet from side to side in a wood. The trees grew close together and were so leafy that he could get no glimpse of the sky. All the light was green light that came through the leaves: but there must have been a very strong sun overhead, for this green daylight was bright and warm. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">站起来时，他注意到，自己不像从水里出来，既不是湿漉漉的，也没有呼吸急促。他的衣服完全是干的。他正站在树林中一个不足十尺宽的小水潭边。那些树密密地长在一起，枝繁叶茂，遮天蔽日。惟一的光线就是从树叶间渗漏下的绿光。然而，树林上面一定是烈日当空，因为那绿光既明亮又温暖。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我回来了，老兄。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 所有东西都买回来了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 除了素汉堡都买回来了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 别告诉我说他们竟没有素汉堡！这算什么快餐店呀！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'm back, buddy.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Did you get everything?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Everything except the vegeburger.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Don't tell me they had no vegeburgers! What sort of fast-food restaurant is it anyway!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There are no ________ to success. It is the result of preparation, hard work, and learning from failure.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">成功没有诀窍。它是用心准备，努力工作，以及从失败中汲取教训的结果。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">secrets</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《亚特兰蒂斯》</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展词链儿：not in the slightest=not at all 毫不，一点</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">儿也不</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>didn't </strong></em></span>seem to mind <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">in the slightest</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他好像<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一点儿都不</strong>在乎。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</strong></span>...hunt for the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">slightest</span></em></strong> misstep in logic or reasoning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...寻找逻辑或推理中<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最微小的</strong>错误。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>But we do not care, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">not in the slightest</span></em></strong> particle of an imaginary thing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但我们不在乎，哪怕是想象出来的东西，我们也<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">毫不</strong>在乎。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">…which helped you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">not</span></em></strong> <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>even</strong></em></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">in the slightest</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">而对自己<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一丁点</strong>好处<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">也没有</strong>的。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ massive adj. 巨大的；强大的，强烈的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">massively adv. 巨大地</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My phone bill was <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">massive</span></em></strong> last month.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">上个月我的电话费数额<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">巨大</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿：in the time continuum 在时间序列中</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">continuum n. 连续体；渐变体；逐渐演变的事物</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">These various complaints are part of a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">continuum</span></em></strong> of ill-health.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这些不同的抱怨是健康<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">连续</strong>欠佳的一部分。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...which is the only thing capable of rupturing the <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>space-time</strong></em></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">continuum</span></em></strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">也是唯一能打破时空<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">连续统一</strong>的物质。</p></section><section 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用 <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">not in the slightest </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was the quietest wood you could possibly imagine. There were no birds, no insects, no animals, and no wind. You could almost feel the trees growing. The pool he had just got out of was not the only pool. There were dozens of others - a pool every few yards as far as his eyes could reach. You could almost feel the trees drinking the water up with their roots. This wood was very much alive. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你可以想像，那是个最为安静的树林，没有鸟，没有虫，没有动物，也没有风。你甚至能感觉到树木在生长。除了他刚才钻出来的那个水潭外，树林里还有不少其他的水潭，极目所视，每隔几步就有一个。你几乎可以感觉到树木用根部在喝水。林子里生机盎然。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我可以跟你谈谈吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 当然，什么事？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我对你最近的工作感到失望。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 对不起，我有一些麻烦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Could I have a word with you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Sure, what is it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I am disappointed with your work lately.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm sorry. I've been having some problems.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He applied the windfall to payment of his mortgage.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他把那笔___________用来偿付抵押。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">意外收入</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 我喜欢“住在船上”这个构想。</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 放弃理性思考</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 对我们而言贵重的东西</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 因为有雾，他们打消了开车去的念头。</strong></p></section></section></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(357px, 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">8.19 早读原文</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">Our brains so hate the idea of losing something </span></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><g style="box-sizing: border-box;">that's</g></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"> valuable to us that we abandon all rational thought, and we make some really poor decisions. </span></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px,
