style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. brain</strong><span style="text-decoration: line-through;color: rgb(0, 82, 255);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">s</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> so 后进同化</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. valuable /ˈvæljuəbəl,  ˈvæljəbəl/ 可四音节，也可三音节</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. th</strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">e i</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">d</strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ea o</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">f 包含两处元元连读加音</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653509148&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=9244116c9ae4132d77cfac4f24b169c6&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="你已选中了添加链接的内容">点击链接跳转回顾【元+元连读小专题】</a></p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1116.91px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 1116.91px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 1116.91px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 1116.91px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. <strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">句式：</strong>so...that... 如此...以至于...</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">so</span></strong></em> weak <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">that</span></em></strong> he could hardly stand up.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他身体虚弱得几乎站不起来了。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Everything happened <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">so</span></em></strong> quickly <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">that</span></em></strong> I hadn’t time to think.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一切都发生得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这么</strong>快，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">都</strong>来不及去思考。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：the idea of doing XX ...的想法/主意</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I had <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">the idea of </span></em></strong>asking Katie for help.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想</strong>请凯蒂帮忙。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I like<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> the idea of</span></em></strong> living on a boat.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我喜欢在船上居住的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">构想</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">注意：不要说 </span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">‘the idea to do <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">something’</g>.</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">而要说 the idea of doing something.</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">或者：it is a good idea to do something</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">以及：it was someone’s idea to do something.</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. abandon v. 抛弃，遗弃；放弃〔信念、信仰或看法〕</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How could she <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">abandon</span></em></strong> her <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">own </g>child?</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她怎么能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">抛弃</strong>自己的孩子呢？</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Because of the <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">fog </g>they <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">abandoned</span></em></strong> their <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">idea of</span></em></strong> driving.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为有雾，他们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">打消了</strong>开车去的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">念头</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">abandon</span></em></strong> it, despite what I said.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">抛弃</strong>它，忘了我说的吧。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6157407" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdvjmW05ZIUpmJqRNXePM74cTGBpiaTyE33CGDkvMLjQ1qXexiblVF6dmPHDQcvickRia19VibLiaXHBqiaA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《爱丽丝梦游仙境》</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You can't just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">abandon</span></em></strong> your son for five months and then show up one day and think that's okay.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">抛下</strong>自己的儿子五个多月之后突然出现还觉得是理所当然。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 2591.69px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 2591.69px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 2591.69px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 2591.69px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.253664" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdvjmW05ZIUpmJqRNXePM74jbAtLMNcqwnggZDJnK02IwttYUQCQBHYobQbA7mw418Rf48Dibcevyw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="887" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《新飞跃比弗利》</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. rational thought 理性的思考</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">logical thought  逻辑思考</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">coherent thought 条理清晰的思考</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was <span style="text-decoration: underline;">so </span>upset <span style="text-decoration: underline;">that</span> he was incapable of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">coherent thought</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他心烦意乱，无法<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">有条理地思考问题</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>Sometimes it's capable of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">rational thought</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有时它能进行<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">理性思考</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>They believed in <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">rational thought</span></em></strong> and experimentation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们相信<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">理性思考</strong>和实验。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There are things in this world that can't be explained by the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">rational mind</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">理性的头脑</strong>并非能解释世间所有事物。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Knows what, though? I mean, what did you really do?</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: I kissed him twice.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than made up for it.</strong></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: So don't do it again? </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: It's not that easy. Every time we're in the same room, it's all we can think about. It's like <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a fog sets with him</strong>, and neither of us can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">see straight</strong>.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: You can't punish people for their thoughts. I'm from China. We've tried.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: I think I should just move. I feel so guilty. I like Camile so much. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: If she knows, she probably just wants to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get it out in the open</strong>. Just go to lunch and maybe avoid anywhere with steak knives.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Sushi's safe. Or anywhere that's Asian. Although if she's mad, a chopstick can puncture skin. Don't ask how I know that.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Can we hang this weekend? I need to not be home.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: My friend Li and her five bridesmaids are in town.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Wedding dress shopping. That sounds fun.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Yeah, um...</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Wait, Why won't a weekend with your friends be fun.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: They're always fun, but <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">their heads would explode if</strong> they knew I was a nanny.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: They're your friends. I'm sure they'll understand. Maybe you should just tell them.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Maybe you should just tell Camile <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're obsessed with</strong> her boyfriend. Sorry. We're going clubbing tonight. Please come. I need a witness to my fake life.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Well, text me details for tonight. I have to plan lunch with my executioner.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: it out in the open”来表达的。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get XX out in the open 坦白；打开天窗说亮话；直说</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let's just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get this out in the open</strong>, okay?</span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">我就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">明说</strong>了？</span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2: </span></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think we kinda<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> get everything out in the open</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我想咱们差不多<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么事都说出来了</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span>“摊牌”还可以怎么说？</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lay one's cards on the table</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Then why don't we skip all that and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lay our cards on the table</strong>?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那何不跳过那部分<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">，把话挑明了说</strong>?</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: rotateZ(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(180deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(180deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section 0);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：I kissed him twice.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than make up for it.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链：</strong>First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than make up for it. 有个一次没事的话，第二次也够够的了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句:</strong> He beat her twice. He should be sent to jail. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than make up for it.  </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他打了她两次，他应该进局子。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">第一次不算，有第二次也够了。</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;line-height: 0;background-color: rgba(86, 61, 227, 0.04);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：They're always fun, but <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">their heads would explode if</strong> they knew I was a nanny.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：XX's head would explode if XX XX要是知道XX就炸锅了<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">My mom's head would explode if </strong>she knew I  was in relationship with him. 我妈要是知道我在跟他谈恋爱就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">炸锅</strong>了。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: border-box;">like </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a fog sets with him</strong>, and neither of us can<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> see straight</strong>.</p><p border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链1</strong>：like a fog sets with XX 看XX雾蒙蒙的；迷迷糊糊的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：When I take off my glasses, it's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">like </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a fog sets with everything</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我摘下眼镜，我看什么都<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">雾蒙蒙</strong>的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链2</strong>：see straight 看清楚</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">see you straight</strong>！Don't bother to get anything from me.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看你看得透透的</strong>，别想从我这得到任何东西。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;line-height: 0;background-color: rgba(86, 61, 227, 0.04);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;">向上滑动阅览</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 5px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E：She knows,right?<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Knows what, though? I mean, what did you really do?</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: I kissed him twice.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than made up for it.</strong></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: So don't do it again? </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: It's not that easy. Every time we're in the same room, it's all we can think about. It's like <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a fog sets with him</strong>, and neither of us can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">see straight</strong>.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: You can't punish people for their thoughts. I'm from China. We've tried.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: I think I should just move. I feel so guilty. I like Camile so much. </p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: If she knows, she probably just wants to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get it out in the open</strong>. Just go to lunch and maybe avoid anywhere with steak knives.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Sushi's safe. Or anywhere that's Asian. Although if she's mad, a chopstick can puncture skin. Don't ask how I know that.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Can we hang this weekend? I need to not be home.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: My friend Li and her five bridesmaids are in town.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Wedding dress shopping. That sounds fun.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Yeah, um...</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Wait, Why won't a weekend with your friends be fun.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: They're always fun, but <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">their heads would explode if</strong> they knew I was a nanny.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: They're your friends. I'm sure they'll understand. Maybe you should just tell them.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">M: Maybe you should just tell Camile <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're obsessed with</strong> her boyfriend. Sorry. We're going clubbing tonight. Please come. I need a witness to my fake life.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E: Well, text me details for tonight. I have to plan lunch with my executioner.</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(156, 156, style="justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 24px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: style="transform: rotateZ(353deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(353deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(353deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(353deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 224, 139);height: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgba(145, 199, 183, 0.24);padding: 25px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 16px;height: 16px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px 0px 0px 1px;border-color: rgb(145, 199, 183) rgb(0, 0, 0) rgb(0, 0, 0) rgb(145, 199, 183);padding: 3px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个段落“摊牌”是用“get it out in the open”来表达的。</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get XX out in the open 坦白；打开天窗说亮话；直说</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let's just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get this out in the open</strong>, okay?</span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">我就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">明说</strong>了？</span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2: </span></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think we kinda<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> get everything out in the open</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我想咱们差不多<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么事都说出来了</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);margin: 10px 0% 3px;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 8px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding: 0px 10px;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: rotateZ(335deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(335deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(335deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(335deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 1px;height: 18px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 29px;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 1px;height: 22px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 8px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span>“摊牌”还可以怎么说？</p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lay one's cards on the table</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px 0px 10px;white-space: normal;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Then why don't we skip all that and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lay our cards on the table</strong>?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那何不跳过那部分<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">，把话挑明了说</strong>?</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: rotateZ(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(180deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(180deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 16px;height: 16px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px 0px 0px 1px;border-color: rgb(145, 199, 183) rgb(0, 0, 0) rgb(0, 0, 0) rgb(145, 199, 183);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 10px 0% 0px;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(233, 245, 254);border-right: 0px none rgb(0, 0, 0);border-top-right-radius: 0px;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;margin: 20px 0% 16px;transform: translate3d(18px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(18px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(18px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(18px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;align-self: flex-end;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 68px;height: 68px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 151px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;align-self: flex-end;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;margin: 0px 0px 0px -38px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-1px, 0px, 0px);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;font-size: 24px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">其它词链儿</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: rotateZ(350deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(350deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(350deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(350deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(255, 224, 139);height: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;margin: -2px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 22px;height: 22px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 151px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;margin: 0px 21px 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 28px 0% 24px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：I kissed him twice.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than make up for it.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链：</strong>First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than make up for it. 有个一次没事的话，第二次也够够的了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句:</strong> He beat her twice. He should be sent to jail. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">First one doesn't count. Well, the second one more than make up for it.  </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他打了她两次，他应该进局子。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">第一次不算，有第二次也够了。</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;line-height: 0;background-color: rgba(86, 61, 227, 0.04);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(119, 95, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-end;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 226, 46);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 28px 0% 24px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：They're always fun, but <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">their heads would explode if</strong> they knew I was a nanny.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：XX's head would explode if XX XX要是知道XX就炸锅了<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">My mom's head would explode if </strong>she knew I  was in relationship with him. 我妈要是知道我在跟他谈恋爱就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">炸锅</strong>了。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;line-height: 0;background-color: rgba(86, 61, 227, 0.04);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(119, 95, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-end;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 226, 46);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 28px 0% 24px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：It's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">like </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a fog sets with him</strong>, and neither of us can<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> see straight</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链1</strong>：like a fog sets with XX 看XX雾蒙蒙的；迷迷糊糊的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：When I take off my glasses, it's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">like </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a fog sets with everything</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我摘下眼镜，我看什么都<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">雾蒙蒙</strong>的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链2</strong>：see straight 看清楚</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">see you straight</strong>！Don't bother to get anything from me.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看你看得透透的</strong>，别想从我这得到任何东西。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;line-height: 0;background-color: rgba(86, 61, 227, 0.04);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;text-align: center;justify-content: center;margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;height: auto;align-self: flex-end;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(119, 95, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 0%;align-self: flex-end;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 8px;height: 8px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 226, 46);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 28px 0% 24px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句：</strong>Maybe you should just tell Camile <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you're obsessed with </strong>her boyfriend.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：be obsessed with XX 沉迷于XX</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：She<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> is obsessed with</strong> the series. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">很喜欢</strong>看那部电视剧。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section border-box;">1. secretly </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈsiːkrɪtli/ adv. 秘密地;</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">if you feel something secretly, you do not tell anyone about your feelings暗暗;暗自</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She secretly nurtured a hope of becoming famous. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她暗暗滋生出成名的愿望。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. strong </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/strɒŋ $ strɒːŋ/ a. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">having a taste or smell that you notice easily醒目的；响亮的；明显感觉得到的；浓烈的；强烈的  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">strong coffee 浓咖啡</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This cheese has a very strong flavour. 这种奶酪味道很浓。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a strong smell of petrol 浓烈的汽油味</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. burn </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/bɜːn $ bɜːrn/ v. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to spoil food by cooking it for too long, or to become spoiled in this way烧焦，烧糊；燃烧;烧;着火;烧着;(使)烧毁，烧坏，烧伤，烧死 n. 烧伤;灼伤;烫伤;烧(或烫、灼)的痕迹;酸痛感;小河;溪流</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">burn something to a crisp/cinder 把...烧焦</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The meat was burned to a crisp. 肉被烧焦了</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. There is +单数可数名词/不可数名词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There are +复数名词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当主语是两个或两个以上的名词时，谓语动词要与跟它最近的那个名词一致。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is a cat and three dogs.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There are three dogs and a cat.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">n egg up to Mrs March</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After Digory had looked at the wood for a long time he noticed that there was a girl lying on her back at the foot of a tree a few yards away. Her eyes were nearly shut but not quite, as if she were just between sleeping and waking. So he looked at her for a long time and said nothing. And at last she opened her eyes and looked at him for a long time and she also said nothing. Then she spoke, in a dreamy, contented sort of voice.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迪格雷久久地注视着那片树林，然后，他发现，离他不远的地方，一个女孩正躺在一棵树下，眼睛微微闭着，似睡非睡的模样。他看了很久，没说话。最后她睁开眼睛，同样看了他良久没有说话。再然后她用梦呓般的心满意足的语调说话了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你看过电影《惊声尖叫》了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 看了。它让我浑身起鸡皮疙瘩。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 算了，哪有那么惨啊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 真的。对我而言，我再也不想看那种电影了</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Have you seen the movie, Scream?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. It gave me the creeps.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Come on, it wasn't that bad.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, it was. As far as I'm concerned, I'm never going to see another movie like that again.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Come on. Be a good sport. You just lost a race.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">算了，做个________的人，你不过输了场比赛。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: Miss Snooty is<span style="background-color: rgb(95, 156, 239);box-sizing: border-box;"> having an affair.</span> Don’t know who the fella is, but she sees him every Tuesday and Friday afternoon at 1:30, <span style="background-color: rgb(95, 156, 239);box-sizing: border-box;">on the dot.</span> Her husband thinks she’s playing bridge, but she’s at the Sunset Palace Hotel. 0.6);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">have some skeleton in one's closet/ have a skeleton in one’s closet</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这句话出自俚语skeleton in the closet，</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直译的话，意思是：柜子里的骷髅，乍听之下，有点害怕。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所谓柜子里的骷髅，意思就是那些见不得人的东西，见不得光的秘密即不可告人的秘密，难言之隐。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Stella never tells us about her past. She must <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">have a skeleton in her closet.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Stella 从来不和我们说她的过去，她肯定<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">有不可告人的秘密。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;letter-spacing: 4px;padding: 0px style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't like to chat with people who<span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="background-color: rgb(96, 156, 239);color: rgb(95, 156, 239);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></span>about others.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可不愿意和那些爱<span style="color: rgb(95, 156, 239);box-sizing: border-box;">说人闲话</span>的人聊天。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br 239);box-sizing: border-box;">dishing the dirt</span> on someone in our class.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那些受欢迎的女生总是在我们班上对别人<span style="color: taxi showed up <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">on the dot.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">出租车<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">准时</span>到了。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Precisely at 12 o'clock <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">on the dot,</span> it is struck.</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时间到达12点<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">整时</span>，大钟敲响。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br against</span> Joan to be president of the Garden Club. powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">have some skeleton in one's closet/ have a skeleton in one’s closet</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这句话出自俚语skeleton in the closet，</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直译的话，意思是：柜子里的骷髅，乍听之下，有点害怕。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所谓柜子里的骷髅，意思就是那些见不得人的东西，见不得光的秘密即不可告人的秘密，难言之隐。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句</p><p style="white-space: border-box;">Stella never tells us about her past. She must <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">have a skeleton in her closet.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Stella 从来不和我们说她的过去，她肯定<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">有不可告人的秘密。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't like to chat with people who<span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span 239);box-sizing: border-box;">dishing the dirt</span> on someone in our class.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那些受欢迎的女生总是在我们班上对别人<span style="color: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: border-box;">have an affair</span>, but not right under my nose.</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">有外遇</span>就有外遇好了，但别在我眼皮底下。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's an open secret that he 's <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">having an affair </span>with his secretary .</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他跟秘书的<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">私情</span>是一个公开的秘密。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span taxi showed up <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">on the dot.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">出租车<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">准时</span>到了。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Precisely at 12 o'clock <span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">on the dot,</span> it is struck.</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时间到达12点<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">整时</span>，大钟敲响。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br He is just a child!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">嘿，别对他说的太<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 0.71);box-sizing: border-box;">直白</span>，他还是个孩子！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: border-box;">blunt</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">太多的酒精使你感觉<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(14, 148, 249, 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">琼尽了最大努力，可土豆的中间还是硬的，蔬菜做得时间太长，变烂了，肉也给烧黑了。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">The strawberries were no</span><span style="text-decoration: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> ready for eating</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> she put sal</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">f sugar</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: them</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 40);box-sizing: border-box;">．</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.20</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What they noticed first was the light. It wasn't like sunlight, and it wasn't like electric light, or lamps, or candles, or any other light they had ever seen. It was a dull,rather red light, not at all cheerful. It was steady and did not flicker. They were standing on a flat paved surface and buildings rose all around them. There was no roofoverhead; they were in a sort of courtyard. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们最先注意到的是光线，既不像日光，也不像电灯、煤油灯、蜡烛或他们见过的任何一种光。那是一种近似红色的惨淡的光，丝毫不让人感到愉快。光线凝固着，没有闪动。他们正站在一个平地上，四面八方都耸立着建筑物。上面没有屋顶，显然是一个院落。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 还记得过去在我们门口那条街上要饭的那个老人吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 记得。他怎么样了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 他找到了一份工作，现在他在城里开了一家小杂货店。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 真不错。我们应该找个时间去看看他。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Remember that old man who used to beg for money on the street across from our house?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yeah. Whatever became of him?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: He got a job and now he owns a small grocery in town.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That's great. We should visit him some time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We need some fresh light on this topic.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个论题上我们需要更多的_________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">新鲜想法</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="text-align:
